config:
    ESXi 5.0 U1 Kickstart ssh:
        cont: "# (c) Copyright 2013, 2014 Hewlett-Packard Development Company, L.P.\n\
            # Accept the VMware End User License Agreement\nvmaccepteula\n \n#-------------------------------------------------------------------------\
            \  \n# Command for server-based licensing\n# To use: Set the Custom Attribute\
            \ for ProductKey_ESXi50 and uncomment the \n#   'vmserialnum' line below\n\
            # vmserialnum --esx=@ProductKey_ESXi50@\n \n# Set the root password for\
            \ the DCUI and Tech Support Mode\nrootpw --iscrypted \"@encrypted_root_password:$1$7z4m7f1z$wliShMhVv2HuCAPmuiQzV1@\"\
            \n \n# Choose the first discovered disk to install onto\n# Note for more\
            \ advanced partitioning, you may want to replace and customize\n# this\
            \ section\ninstall --firstdisk --overwritevmfs\n \n# reboot after installation\n\
            reboot\n \n# Set the network to DHCP on the network adapater\nnetwork\
            \ --bootproto=dhcp\n\n## first boot\n%firstboot --interpreter=busybox\n\
            vim-cmd hostsvc/enable_ssh\nvim-cmd hostsvc/start_ssh\nvim-cmd hostsvc/enable_esx_shell\n\
            vim-cmd hostsvc/start_esx_shell\n \n## post-install script\n### DO NOT\
            \ MODIFY THE CODE BELOW. IT WILL RESULT IN BUILD PLAN FAILURE ###\n%post\
            \ --interpreter=python --ignorefailure=true\nimport time\nstampFile =\
            \ file(\"/finished.stamp\", mode=\"w\")\nstampFile.write( time.asctime()\
            \ )\n"
        desc: 'Answer file for the specified OS.


            Optional Custom Attributes:

            * encrypted_root_password

            * kernel_arguments

            * ProductKey_ESXi50 - Requires editing answer file to remove the comment
            for the vmserionum line.'

    RHEL 5.10 x64 en_us Kickstart GUI:
        cont: "# (c) Copyright 2014 Hewlett-Packard Development Company, L.P.\nlang\
            \ en_US\nkeyboard us\ntimezone --utc America/Chicago\ntext\ninstall\n\
            key --skip\nxconfig --startxonboot\nnetwork  --bootproto dhcp\n \n \n\
            authconfig --enableshadow --enablemd5\nrootpw --iscrypted \"@encrypted_root_password:$1$7z4m7f1z$wliShMhVv2HuCAPmuiQzV1@\"\
            \n \nzerombr\nclearpart --all --initlabel\nautopart\n \nbootloader --append=\"\
            @kernel_arguments: @\" --location=mbr\n \n# Disable firewall and selinux\
            \ for SPP components\nfirewall --disabled\n# Port 1002 is needed for agent\
            \ communication if the firewall is enabled\n# firewall --enable --port=1002:tcp\n\
            selinux --disabled\n \n%packages\n@Base\n@ Core\n@ Administration Tools\n\
            @ Legacy Software Support\n@ System Tools\n@ DNS Name Server\n@ Legacy\
            \ Network Server\n@ Network Servers\n@ Server Configuration Tools\n@ Development\
            \ Tools\n@ FTP Server\n@ GNOME Desktop Environment\n@ GNOME Software Development\n\
            @ X Window System\n@ Graphical Internet\nlm_sensors\nlibnl\n \n# Components\
            \ listed below are needed to run HPSUM and SPP components\nlibICE.i386\n\
            libSM.i386\nlibXau.i386\nlibXdmcp.i386\nlibX11.i386\nlibXrender.i386\n\
            freetype.i386\nfontconfig.i386\nlibXext.i386\n \nmake\nnet-snmp\nnet-snmp-libs\n"
        desc: 'Answer file for the specified OS.


            Optional Custom Attributes:

            * encrypted_root_password

            * kernel_arguments'

        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --maintenance --atLeast=3 --atMost=20

    CSI Custom - Install Linux Gen9Snap3 SPP build 106:
        attr: []
        desc: 'Installs the Service Pack for ProLiant (SPP) on a Linux production
            target server.

            (c) Copyright 2013, 2014 Hewlett-Packard Development Company, L.P.


            Requirements:

            * HP ProLiant server with iLO running a Linux production OS

            * IC server provisioning Media Server must contain a SPP


            Optional Custom Attribute:  None'
        steps:
        -   name: Check iLO Service
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Set Media Source
            para: '@__OPSW-Media-WinUser@@__OPSW-Media-WinPassword@@__OPSW-Media-WinPath@#/mnt/media?noserverino'
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Install Linux SPP
            para: --spp_version=@SPPversion:Gen9Snap3@ --hpsum_options="-use_wmi -use_snmp
                -use_ams"
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Reboot
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --production --atLeast=3 --atMost=30
            type: ogfsScripts
        type: SW - Firmware

        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --production --atLeast=2 --atMost=60
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Report Windows SPP Installation Results
            para: ''
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Reboot
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --production --atLeast=3 --atMost=30
            type: ogfsScripts
        type: SW - Firmware

    CSI Custom - Intelligent Provisioning 1.62 Firmware Update:
        attr: []
        desc: "Updates the Intelligent Provisioning firmware while booted to PXE Linux\
            \ service OS.\n(c) Copyright 2014 Hewlett-Packard Development Company,\
            \ L.P.\n\nRequirements:\n* HP ProLiant Gen8 server or newer \n* IC server\
            \ provisioning Media Server must contain Intelligent Provisioning media\n\
            * Network must support PXE boot of server"
        steps:
        -   name: Check iLO Service
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Verify Supported Boot Modes
            para: --secure=disabled
            type: ogfsScripts

            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Boot
            para: --serviceOS=linux64 --method=network --force
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --maintenance --atLeast=3 --atMost=20
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Set Media Source
            para: '@__OPSW-Media-WinUser@@__OPSW-Media-WinPassword@@__OPSW-Media-WinPath@#/mnt/media?noserverino'
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: LinuxPE add-on packages
            para: /
            type: packages
        -   name: Update Intelligent Provisioning Firmware
            para: --ip_version=@IPversion:1.62@
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Boot
            para: --serviceOS=linux64 --force
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --maintenance --atLeast=3 --atMost=20
            type: ogfsScripts
        type: SW - Firmware

    CSI Custom - RHEL 5.10 x64 Scripted GUI Install:
        attr: []
        desc: 'Performs a scripted install of Red Hat Enterprise Linux 5.10 using
            a generic kickstart file.

            (c) Copyright 2014, 2015 Hewlett-Packard Development Company, L.P.


            Requirements:

            * HP ProLiant server with iLO

            * IC server provisioning Media Server must contain the OS distribution


            Required Custom Attributes:  None


            Optional Custom Attributes:

            * encrypted_root_password (must be encrypted)

            * boot_disk

            * kernel_arguments


            Note: No new RHEL 5.10 drivers are available after 2014.06.0.'
        steps:
        -   name: Check iLO Service
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Verify Supported Boot Modes
            para: --uefi=false
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Boot
            para: --serviceOS=linux64
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Decommission Server
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --maintenance --atLeast=3 --atMost=20
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Set Media Source
            para: '@__OPSW-Media-LinURI@/rhel510-x64'
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: RHEL 5.10 x64 en_us Kickstart GUI
            para: /tmp/user.ks.cfg
            type: configs
        -   name: Inject Required Kickstart Settings
            para: Red Hat Enterprise Linux Server 5 X86_64
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Inject Kickstart Personalization Settings
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Create Stub Partition
            para: ''
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Copy Boot Media
            para: ''
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: ProLiant Drivers for RHEL 5.10 x64 - 2014.06.0
            para: ''
            type: packages
        -   name: GRuB Boot Loader x86
            para: ''
            type: packages
        -   name: Deploy Agent
            para: -d /tmp/opt/opsware/agent/ogfs-agent.zip -u
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Embed files initrd
            para: -s /tmp/user.ks.cfg:/ -s /tmp/opt/opsware/agent:/opt/opsware/ -s
                /tmp/dud/.:/
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Install bootloader for RedHat Enterprise Linux Server
            para: --kernel_arguments="@kernel_arguments@"
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Reboot
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --maintenance --atLeast=3 --atMost=20
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Monitor Installation
            para: tmp/anaconda.log
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Integrate Linux HP SA Agent
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Reboot
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --production --atLeast=3 --atMost=30
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Personalize Network Settings of Installed System
            para: ''
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --production
            type: ogfsScripts
        type: OS - Red Hat Enterprise Linux Server 5

    CSI Custom - Windows 2012 Datacenter x64 Scripted Install with SNMP Configuration:
        attr: []
        desc: 'Performs a scripted install of Windows 2012 Standard using a generic
            unattend file.

            (c) Copyright 2013-2015 Hewlett-Packard Development Company, L.P.


            Requirements:

            * HP ProLiant server with iLO

            * IC server provisioning Media Server must contain the OS distribution


            Required Custom Attribute:

            * ProductKey_Win2012-Std-x64 - Set using the Settings -> Product Key page.


            Optional Custom Attributes:

            * ComputerName

            * EncryptedAdminPassword (must be encrypted)

            * SystemDisk

            * SystemDiskNumber'
        steps:
        -   name: Validate Custom Attributes
            para: --custAttrNames "ProductKey_Win2012-Std-x64"
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Check iLO Service
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Verify Supported Boot Modes
            para: --secure=disabled
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Boot
            para: --serviceOS=winpe64
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Decommission Server
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --maintenance --atLeast=3 --atMost=20
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Prepare Disks on HP ProLiant Gen8
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Install and boot into local WinPE
            para: --systemDiskNumber=@SystemDiskNumber:0@ --systemDrive=@SystemDrive:c@
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Set Media Source
            para: '@__OPSW-Media-WinUser@@__OPSW-Media-WinPassword@@__OPSW-Media-WinPath@#z'
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Configure Windows Partitioning Scheme for Legacy
            para: X:\Windows\Temp\diskpart_legacy.txt
            type: configs
        -   name: Configure Windows Partitioning Scheme for Uefi
            para: X:\Windows\Temp\diskpart_uefi.txt
            type: configs
        -   name: Partition Disk for Windows
            para: --systemDiskNumber=@SystemDiskNumber:0@
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Windows 2012 DataCenter x64 en_us Unattend SNMP Config
            para: x:\Windows\Temp\Unattend.xml
            type: configs
        -   name: Inject Required Unattend.xml Settings
            para: --WindowsPartitionID=Autodetect
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Inject Personalization Settings
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: ProLiant Drivers for Windows 2012 - 2015.06.0
            para: '@SystemDrive:c@:\$oem$'
            type: packages
        -   name: Run Windows 2012 x64 Setup
            para: '"z:\Media\win2012-x64-en_us\setup.exe"'
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Integrate HP SA Agent
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Reboot
            para: ''
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --production --atLeast=3 --atMost=30
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: Personalize Network Settings of Installed System
            para: ''
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --production --atLeast=3 --atMost=30
            type: ogfsScripts
        -   name: SNMP options-Accept SNMP packets from any host
            para: ''
            type: serverScripts
        -   name: Wait for HP SA Agent
            para: --production
            type: ogfsScripts
        type: OS - Windows Server 2012

    Add Windows features and roles for NIC team:
        cont: "@echo off\n\n:: (c) Copyright 2013, 2014 Hewlett-Packard Development\
            \ Company, L.P.\n\nset wdir=%windir%\nset FEATURE=Web-Server -IncludeManagementTools\n\
            set FEATURE1=Multipath-IO -IncludeManagementTools\nset FEATURE4=NET-Framework-Features\
            \ -IncludeManagementTools\nset FEATURE5=hyper-V -IncludeManagementTools\
            \ -Restart\nset RESULTFILE=\"%wdir%\\FeatureInstallResult.xml\"\n\n::\
            \ Try PowerShell if exists\nfor %%X in (powershell.exe) do (set FOUND1=%%~$PATH:X)\n\
            if defined FOUND1 (\n   echo Import-module servermanager > \"%wdir%\\\
            FeatureInstall.ps1\"\n   echo add-windowsfeature -Name %FEATURE% -logPath\
            \ %RESULTFILE% >> \"%wdir%\\FeatureInstall.ps1\"\n   echo add-windowsfeature\
            \ -Name %FEATURE1% -logPath %RESULTFILE% >> \"%wdir%\\FeatureInstall.ps1\"\
            \n   echo add-windowsfeature -Name %FEATURE4% -logPath %RESULTFILE% >>\
            \ \"%wdir%\\FeatureInstall.ps1\"\n   echo add-windowsfeature -Name %FEATURE5%\
            \ -logPath %RESULTFILE% >> \"%wdir%\\FeatureInstall.ps1\"\n   powershell.exe\
            \ -ExecutionPolicy Unrestricted -NoLogo -NonInteractive -NoProfile -WindowStyle\
            \ Hidden -File \"%wdir%\\FeatureInstall.ps1\"\n   set rc=%errorlevel%\n\
            \   goto EndWithFailureMessage\n)\n\n:: Try ServerManagerCmd if exists\
            \ and PowerShell wasn't found\nfor %%X in (ServerManagerCmd.exe) do (set\
            \ FOUND2=%%~$PATH:X)\nif defined FOUND2 (\n   ServerManagerCmd.exe -install\
            \ %FEATURE% -resultPath %RESULTFILE% >> %temp%\\status.log\n   set rc=%errorlevel%\n\
            \   goto EndWithFailureMessage\n) \n\nif NOT defined rc (\n   echo PowerShell\
            \ and ServerManagerCmd were not found and could not set %FEATURE%\n  \
            \ set rc=99\n   goto End\n)\n\n:EndWithFailureMessage\nif NOT %rc%==0\
            \ (\n   echo PowerShell and ServerManagerCmd Add Windows Feature failed\
            \ to install %FEATURE%:  error code %rc%\n   echo Refer to %RESULTFILE%\
            \ log file.\n)\n\n:End\nexit /B %rc%\n"
        desc: 'Installs the Windows Hyper-V Role using ServerManagerCmd or PowerShell
            on a Windows production OS.  A reboot is required after this script is
            run.


            Parameters:  None


            Custom Attributes: None'
        sudo: false
        type: BAT
    Configure snmpd.conf:
        cont: "mkdir -p /etc/snmp/\ncat > /etc/snmp/snmpd.conf << EOF\n# Following\
            \ entries were added by HP Insight Management Agents at\n#      Thu Apr\
            \ 30 12:56:43 CDT 2015\ndlmod cmaX /usr/lib64/libcmaX64.so\nrwcommunity\
            \ public 127.0.0.1\nrocommunity public 127.0.0.1\nrwcommunity  public\
            \ 0.0.0.0\nrocommunity  public 0.0.0.0\ntrapcommunity public\ntrapsink\
            \ 127.0.0.1 public\nsyscontact Root <root@localhost> (configure /etc/snmp/snmp.local.conf)\n\
            syslocation lab (edit /etc/snmp/snmpd.conf)\n\n# ----------------------\
            \ END --------------------\n###############################################################################\n\
            #\n# snmpd.conf:\n#   An example configuration file for configuring the\
            \ ucd-snmp snmpd agent.\n#\n###############################################################################\n\
            #\n# This file is intended to only be as a starting point.  Many more\n\
            # configuration directives exist than are mentioned in this file.  For\
            \ \n# full details, see the snmpd.conf(5) manual page.\n#\n# All lines\
            \ beginning with a '#' are comments and are intended for you\n# to read.\
            \  All other lines are configuration commands for the agent.\n\n###############################################################################\n\
            # Access Control\n###############################################################################\n\
            \n# As shipped, the snmpd demon will only respond to queries on the\n\
            # system mib group until this file is replaced or modified for\n# security\
            \ purposes.  Examples are shown below about how to increase the\n# level\
            \ of access.\n\n# By far, the most common question I get about the agent\
            \ is \"why won't\n# it work?\", when really it should be \"how do I configure\
            \ the agent to\n# allow me to access it?\"\n#\n# By default, the agent\
            \ responds to the \"public\" community for read\n# only access, if run\
            \ out of the box without any configuration file in \n# place.  The following\
            \ examples show you other ways of configuring\n# the agent so that you\
            \ can change the community names, and give\n# yourself write access to\
            \ the mib tree as well.\n#\n# For more information, read the FAQ as well\
            \ as the snmpd.conf(5)\n# manual page.\n\n####\n# First, map the community\
            \ name \"public\" into a \"security name\"\n\n#       sec.name  source\
            \          community\ncom2sec notConfigUser  default       public\n\n\
            ####\n# Second, map the security name into a group name:\n\n#       groupName\
            \      securityModel securityName\ngroup   notConfigGroup v1         \
            \  notConfigUser\ngroup   notConfigGroup v2c           notConfigUser\n\
            \n####\n# Third, create a view for us to let the group have rights to:\n\
            \n# Make at least  snmpwalk -v 1 localhost -c public system fast again.\n\
            #       name           incl/excl     subtree         mask(optional)\n\
            view    systemview    included   .1.3.6.1.2.1.1\nview    systemview  \
            \  included   .1.3.6.1.2.1.25.1.1\n\n####\n# Finally, grant the group\
            \ read-only access to the systemview view.\n\n#       group          context\
            \ sec.model sec.level prefix read   write  notif\naccess  notConfigGroup\
            \ \"\"      any       noauth    exact  systemview none none\n\n# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\
            \n# Here is a commented out example configuration that allows less\n#\
            \ restrictive access.\n\n# YOU SHOULD CHANGE THE \"COMMUNITY\" TOKEN BELOW\
            \ TO A NEW KEYWORD ONLY\n# KNOWN AT YOUR SITE.  YOU *MUST* CHANGE THE\
            \ NETWORK TOKEN BELOW TO\n# SOMETHING REFLECTING YOUR LOCAL NETWORK ADDRESS\
            \ SPACE.\n\n##       sec.name  source          community\n#com2sec local\
            \     localhost       COMMUNITY\n#com2sec mynetwork NETWORK/24      COMMUNITY\n\
            \n##     group.name sec.model  sec.name\n#group MyRWGroup  any       \
            \ local\n#group MyROGroup  any        mynetwork\n#\n#group MyRWGroup \
            \ any        otherv3user\n#...\n\n##           incl/excl subtree     \
            \                     mask\n#view all    included  .1                \
            \               80\n\n## -or just the mib2 tree-\n\n#view mib2   included\
            \  .iso.org.dod.internet.mgmt.mib-2 fc\n\n\n##                context\
            \ sec.model sec.level prefix read   write  notif\n#access MyROGroup \"\
            \"      any       noauth    0      all    none   none\n#access MyRWGroup\
            \ \"\"      any       noauth    0      all    all    all\n\n\n###############################################################################\n\
            # Sample configuration to make net-snmpd RFC 1213.\n# Unfortunately v1\
            \ and v2c don't allow any user based authentification, so\n# opening up\
            \ the default config is not an option from a security point.\n#\n# WARNING:\
            \ If you uncomment the following lines you allow write access to your\n\
            # snmpd daemon from any source! To avoid this use different names for\
            \ your\n# community or split out the write access to a different community\
            \ and \n# restrict it to your local network.\n# otherwise they are still\
            \ read only (see FAQ for net-snmp).\n#\n\n# First, map the community name\
            \ \"public\" into a \"security name\"\n#       sec.name        source\
            \          community\n#com2sec notConfigUser   default         public\n\
            \n# Second, map the security name into a group name:\n#       groupName\
            \       securityModel   securityName\n#group   notConfigGroup  v1    \
            \          notConfigUser\n#group   notConfigGroup  v2c             notConfigUser\n\
            \n# Third, create a view for us to let the group have rights to:\n# Open\
            \ up the whole tree for ro, make the RFC 1213 required ones rw.\n#   \
            \    name            incl/excl       subtree mask(optional)\n#view   \
            \ roview          included        .1\n#view    rwview          included\
            \        system.sysContact\n#view    rwview          included        system.sysName\n\
            #view    rwview          included        system.sysLocation\n#view   \
            \ rwview          included        interfaces.ifTable.ifEntry.ifAdminStatus\n\
            #view    rwview          included        at.atTable.atEntry.atPhysAddress\n\
            #view    rwview          included        at.atTable.atEntry.atNetAddress\n\
            #view    rwview          included        ip.ipForwarding\n#view    rwview\
            \          included        ip.ipDefaultTTL\n#view    rwview          included\
            \        ip.ipRouteTable.ipRouteEntry.ipRouteDest\n#view    rwview   \
            \       included        ip.ipRouteTable.ipRouteEntry.ipRouteIfIndex\n\
            #view    rwview          included        ip.ipRouteTable.ipRouteEntry.ipRouteMetric1\n\
            #view    rwview          included        ip.ipRouteTable.ipRouteEntry.ipRouteMetric2\n\
            #view    rwview          included        ip.ipRouteTable.ipRouteEntry.ipRouteMetric3\n\
            #view    rwview          included        ip.ipRouteTable.ipRouteEntry.ipRouteMetric4\n\
            #view    rwview          included        ip.ipRouteTable.ipRouteEntry.ipRouteType\n\
            #view    rwview          included        ip.ipRouteTable.ipRouteEntry.ipRouteAge\n\
            #view    rwview          included        ip.ipRouteTable.ipRouteEntry.ipRouteMask\n\
            #view    rwview          included        ip.ipRouteTable.ipRouteEntry.ipRouteMetric5\n\
            #view    rwview          included        ip.ipNetToMediaTable.ipNetToMediaEntry.ipNetToMediaIfIndex\n\
            #view    rwview          included        ip.ipNetToMediaTable.ipNetToMediaEntry.ipNetToMediaPhysAddress\n\
            #view    rwview          included        ip.ipNetToMediaTable.ipNetToMediaEntry.ipNetToMediaNetAddress\n\
            #view    rwview          included        ip.ipNetToMediaTable.ipNetToMediaEntry.ipNetToMediaType\n\
            #view    rwview          included        tcp.tcpConnTable.tcpConnEntry.tcpConnState\n\
            #view    rwview          included        egp.egpNeighTable.egpNeighEntry.egpNeighEventTrigger\n\
            #view    rwview          included        snmp.snmpEnableAuthenTraps\n\n\
            # Finally, grant the group read-only access to the systemview view.\n\
            #       group          context sec.model sec.level prefix read   write\
            \  notif\n#access  notConfigGroup \"\"      any       noauth    exact\
            \  roview rwview none\n\n\n\n###############################################################################\n\
            # System contact information\n#\n\n# It is also possible to set the sysContact\
            \ and sysLocation system\n# variables through the snmpd.conf file:\n\n\
            \n# Example output of snmpwalk:\n#   % snmpwalk -v 1 localhost -c public\
            \ system\n#   system.sysDescr.0 = \"SunOS name sun4c\"\n#   system.sysObjectID.0\
            \ = OID: enterprises.ucdavis.ucdSnmpAgent.sunos4\n#   system.sysUpTime.0\
            \ = Timeticks: (595637548) 68 days, 22:32:55\n#   system.sysContact.0\
            \ = \"Me <me@somewhere.org>\"\n#   system.sysName.0 = \"name\"\n#   system.sysLocation.0\
            \ = \"Right here, right now.\"\n#   system.sysServices.0 = 72\n\n\n###############################################################################\n\
            # Logging\n#\n\n# We do not want annoying \"Connection from UDP: \" messages\
            \ in syslog.\n# If the following option is commented out, snmpd will print\
            \ each incoming\n# connection, which can be useful for debugging.\n\n\
            dontLogTCPWrappersConnects yes\n\n# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\
            \n\n###############################################################################\n\
            # Process checks.\n#\n#  The following are examples of how to use the\
            \ agent to check for\n#  processes running on the host.  The syntax looks\
            \ something like:\n#\n#  proc NAME [MAX=0] [MIN=0]\n#\n#  NAME:  the name\
            \ of the process to check for.  It must match\n#         exactly (ie,\
            \ http will not find httpd processes).\n#  MAX:   the maximum number allowed\
            \ to be running.  Defaults to 0.\n#  MIN:   the minimum number to be running.\
            \  Defaults to 0.\n\n#\n#  Examples (commented out by default):\n#\n\n\
            #  Make sure mountd is running\n#proc mountd\n\n#  Make sure there are\
            \ no more than 4 ntalkds running, but 0 is ok too.\n#proc ntalkd 4\n\n\
            #  Make sure at least one sendmail, but less than or equal to 10 are running.\n\
            #proc sendmail 10 1\n\n#  A snmpwalk of the process mib tree would look\
            \ something like this:\n# \n# % snmpwalk -v 1 localhost -c public .1.3.6.1.4.1.2021.2\n\
            # enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prIndex.1 = 1\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prIndex.2\
            \ = 2\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prIndex.3 = 3\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prNames.1\
            \ = \"mountd\"\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prNames.2 = \"\
            ntalkd\"\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prNames.3 = \"sendmail\"\
            \n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prMin.1 = 0\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prMin.2\
            \ = 0\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prMin.3 = 1\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prMax.1\
            \ = 0\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prMax.2 = 4\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prMax.3\
            \ = 10\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prCount.1 = 0\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prCount.2\
            \ = 0\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prCount.3 = 1\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prErrorFlag.1\
            \ = 1\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prErrorFlag.2 = 0\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prErrorFlag.3\
            \ = 0\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prErrMessage.1 = \"No mountd\
            \ process running.\"\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prErrMessage.2\
            \ = \"\"\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prErrMessage.3 = \"\"\
            \n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prErrFix.1 = 0\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prErrFix.2\
            \ = 0\n# enterprises.ucdavis.procTable.prEntry.prErrFix.3 = 0\n#\n#  Note\
            \ that the errorFlag for mountd is set to 1 because one is not\n#  running\
            \ (in this case an rpc.mountd is, but thats not good enough),\n#  and\
            \ the ErrMessage tells you what's wrong.  The configuration\n#  imposed\
            \ in the snmpd.conf file is also shown.  \n# \n#  Special Case:  When\
            \ the min and max numbers are both 0, it assumes\n#  you want a max of\
            \ infinity and a min of 1.\n#\n\n\n# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\
            \n\n###############################################################################\n\
            # Executables/scripts\n#\n\n#\n#  You can also have programs run by the\
            \ agent that return a single\n#  line of output and an exit code.  Here\
            \ are two examples.\n#\n#  exec NAME PROGRAM [ARGS ...]\n#\n#  NAME: \
            \    A generic name. The name must be unique for each exec statement.\n\
            #  PROGRAM:  The program to run.  Include the path!\n#  ARGS:     optional\
            \ arguments to be passed to the program\n\n# a simple hello world\n\n\
            #exec echotest /bin/echo hello world\n\n# Run a shell script containing:\n\
            #\n# #!/bin/sh\n# echo hello world\n# echo hi there\n# exit 35\n#\n# Note:\
            \  this has been specifically commented out to prevent\n# accidental security\
            \ holes due to someone else on your system writing\n# a /tmp/shtest before\
            \ you do.  Uncomment to use it.\n#\n#exec shelltest /bin/sh /tmp/shtest\n\
            \n# Then, \n# % snmpwalk -v 1 localhost -c public .1.3.6.1.4.1.2021.8\n\

    Install Linux SPP Copy:
        cont: "#!/bin/sh\n\n# (c) Copyright 2013, 2014 Hewlett-Packard Development\
            \ Company, L.P.\n\n# Globals\n# Media Server mount point location\n# if\
            \ /mnt/media not exist fall back to /mnt/ms mount point\nmountpoint=/mnt/media\n\
            if [ ! -d \"$mountpoint\" ]\nthen\n\tmountpoint=/mnt/ms\nfi\n\nhpsumargs=\n\
            sppversion=\n\n#Flag to be used in case --fail_on_warning is specified.\n\
            failonwarning=0\n#Flag to be used in case -logdir is specified.\nlogdir_specified=0\n\
            #Variable to save the new logdir specified.\nnew_logdir=\"/var/hp/log\"\
            \n\n# ====================\n# Determine SPP Version to install\n# Globals\
            \ set:  sppversion\n# ====================\nFindSPPVersion ()\n{     \
            \  \n   if [ \"$sppversion\" == \"\" ] || [ \"$sppversion\" == \"latest\"\
            \ ]; then\n\n      sppversion=$(find \"$mountpoint/Media/spp\" -mindepth\
            \ 1 -maxdepth 1 -type d -printf %f\\\\n | sort | tail -1)\n\n      if\
            \ [ \"$sppversion\" == \"\" ]; then\n         echo \"Did not find an SPP\
            \ Version on the media server\"\n         return 999\n      fi\n     \
            \ if [ ! -d \"$mountpoint/Media/spp/$sppversion\" ]; then\n         echo\
            \ \"$mountpoint/Media/spp/$sppversion is not a directory\"\n         return\
            \ 999\n      fi\n   fi\n   return 0\n}\n\n# ====================\n# Run\
            \ HPSUM\n# Globals used:  hpsumargs, sppversion\n# ====================\n\
            RunHPSUM ()\n{\n   if [ ! -d \"$mountpoint/Media/spp/$sppversion\" ];\
            \ then\n      echo \"$mountpoint/Media/spp/$sppversion does not exist\"\
            \n      return 999\n   fi\n\n   echo \"SPP version to be installed is\
            \ $sppversion\"\n   echo \"Additional hpsum arguments are $hpsumargs\"\
            \n   # Must be run as currently running directory\n   cd $mountpoint/Media/spp/$sppversion/hp/swpackages\n\
            \n   ./hpsum --silent $hpsumargs\n   rc=$?\n    if [ $rc -gt 3 ] || [\
            \ $rc -lt 0 ]; then\n        echo \"SPP hpsum failed: error code $rc\"\
            \n        if [[ $rc -lt 0 ]]; then\n            rc=$(( 256 + $rc ))\n\
            \        fi\n      \t  case \"$rc\" in\n\t      255)\n    \t\t  echo \"\
            A general failure occurred. For details, see the error log.\";;\n\t  \
            \    254)\n    \t\t  echo \"A bad input parameter was encountered.\";;\n\
            \              253)\n                  if [ $failonwarning -eq 1 ];then\n\
            \t\t\techo \"ERROR - One or more components failed to install\"\n    \
            \                    echo \"fail_on_warning is set\"\n       \t\t  else\n\
            \t\t\techo \"WARNING - One or more of the smart components failed to install.\"\
            \n\t\t\techo \"Depending on your system configuration, this may be expected\
            \ behavior.\"\n\t\t\techo \"To verify the installation, check the hpsum\
            \ logs located at $new_logdir unless specified otherwise by hpsum -logdir\
            \ option.\"\n\t\t\techo \"To fail the build plan when these warnings occur,\
            \ specify the --fail_on_warning option to this step.\"\n\t\t\treturn 0\n\
            \t\t  fi\n\t\t\t;;\n\t  esac\n    \n    echo \"hpsum logs are located\
            \ at $new_logdir unless specified otherwise by hpsum -logdir option.\"\
            \n    return $rc\n    fi\n    if [ $rc -ge 0 ] || [ $rc -le 3 ]; then\n\
            \        case \"$rc\" in\n\t      0)\n    \t\t  echo \"SPP hpsum ran successfully:\
            \ return code $rc\";;\n\t      1)\n    \t\t  echo \"The installation was\
            \ successful,but a reboot is required: return code $rc\";;\n         \
            \     3)\n    \t\t  echo \"The component was current or not required:\
            \ return code $rc\";;\n\tesac\n    \n    echo \"hpsum logs are located\
            \ at $new_logdir unless specified otherwise by hpsum -logdir option.\"\
            \n    return 0\n    fi\n}\n\n# ====================\n# Unmount media server\n\
            # Globals used:  mountpoint\n# ====================\nUnmountMediaServer()\n\
            {\n   # Unmount media server drive\n   cd /\n   umount \"$mountpoint\"\
            \n   return 0\n}\n\n# ====================\n# MAIN\n# ====================\n\
            \n# Determine what calling arguments\n# Globals set:  hpsumargs, sppversion\n\
            \nopt=0\nfor i in $*\ndo\n    # Get string to left of =\n    leftstr=${i%=*}\n\
            \    # Get string to right of =\n    rightstr=${i##*=}\n    case \"$leftstr\"\
            \ in\n        \"--spp_version\")\n            sppversion=$rightstr;;\n\
            \    \"--hpsum_options\")\n        hpsumargs=$rightstr;;\n    \"--fail_on_warning\"\
            )\n       failonwarning=1;;\n    *)\n        if [ $i == \"-logdir\" ];then\n\
            \            logdir_specified=1\n            hpsumargs=\"$hpsumargs $i\"\
            \n        elif [ $logdir_specified -eq 1 ]; then\n            hpsumargs=\"\
            $hpsumargs \\\"$i\\\"\"\n            new_logdir=\"\\\"$i\\\"\"\n     \
            \       logdir_specified=0\n        else\n            hpsumargs=\"$hpsumargs\
            \ $i\"\n        fi\n        ;;\n    esac\ndone\n\n\nFindSPPVersion\nreturncode=$?\n\
            \nif [ $returncode -eq 0 ]; then\n    RunHPSUM\n    returncode=$?\nfi\n\
            UnmountMediaServer\n\nexit $returncode\n"
        desc: "Installs the HP Service Pack for ProLiant on Linux production OS using\
            \ the HP SUM utility and specified SPP version.\n\nOptional Parameters:\n\
            --spp_version=directory_name    The name of the directory containing the\
            \ SPP to be installed, such as \"2014.02.0\".  If the value is blank or\
            \ \"latest\", the script automatically selects the directory with the\
            \ latest version as determined by sort order.\n\n--hpsum_options=\"option1\
            \ option2 option3 ... optionN\"    HP SUM supported command-line options\
            \ that are to be passed to HP SUM.  Refer to HP SUM's CLIhelp.txt documentation\
            \ file for available options.\n\n--fail_on_warning : When specified, the\
            \ script will fail on receiving the error code 253. When absent, the script\
            \ will be successful for the error code 253. \n\nRequirements:\n* Media\
            \ Server mounted with Set Media Source script.\n* The directories containing\
            \ the SPPs must reside on the Media Server under the \"\\Media\\spp\"\
            \ directory.\n\nCustom Attributes: None"
        sudo: true
        type: SH
